*Matěj Boxan,William Larivée-Hardy,François Pomerleau*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文评估了三种现有旋转FMCW雷达里程计方法在高动态地形（如亚北极环境）下的表现，并提出一种结合惯性测量的新方法，在动态轨迹下效果优异。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统雷达里程计假设地面平坦，但亚北极等复杂地形变化剧烈，原有方法在特征提取和状态估计上表现不佳。为提升此类环境下的导航准确性，需要探索更鲁棒的解决方案。

Method: 论文在高动态地形（俯仰角达30°、横滚达8°）下，基准测试了三种雷达里程计方法。同时，提出了一种融合雷达与惯性信息的创新方法：利用倾斜-邻近子地图搜索和垂直位移硬阈值来提升点云配准精度。

Result: 新方法在城市基线数据集上达到最先进水平，在动态2公里轨迹测试中相较于第二优方法提升了0.3%。此外，四种方法在侧滑大和陡沟环境下的表现差异也被详细分析。

Conclusion: 融合型雷达-惯性里程计方法在多变复杂地形表现优越，为高动态环境下的精确导航提供了新的技术路线。

Abstract: Rotating FMCW radar odometry methods often assume flat ground conditions. While this assumption is sufficient in many scenarios, including urban environments or flat mining setups, the highly dynamic terrain of subarctic environments poses a challenge to standard feature extraction and state estimation techniques. This paper benchmarks three existing radar odometry methods under demanding conditions, exhibiting up to 13° in pitch and 4° in roll difference between consecutive scans, with absolute pitch and roll reaching 30° and 8°, respectively. Furthermore, we propose a novel radar-inertial odometry method utilizing tilt-proximity submap search and a hard threshold for vertical displacement between scan points and the estimated axis of rotation. Experimental results demonstrate a state-of-the-art performance of our method on an urban baseline and a 0.3% improvement over the second-best comparative method on a 2-kilometer-long dynamic trajectory. Finally, we analyze the performance of the four evaluated methods on a complex radar sequence characterized by high lateral slip and a steep ditch traversal.

</details>


### [171] [Efficient Reinforcement Learning using Linear Koopman Dynamics for Nonlinear Robotic Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.19980)
*Wenjian Hao,Yuxuan Fang,Zehui Lu,Shaoshuai Mou*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于模型的强化学习方法，用于非线性机器人系统的最优闭环控制，并通过与传统和主流方法的对比，展示了在多个平台上的优越性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 非线性机器人系统的闭环最优控制具有高度挑战性，现有无模型或有模型强化学习方法在样本效率与控制性能上均有不足。本文动机在于利用Koopman算子理论，将非线性系统升维线性化，结合高效的策略优化，弥补现有方法的不足，并兼顾理论与实际落地。

Method: 通过Koopman算子理论学习线性升维动力学，将学习到的动力学模型结合到actor-critic架构中，仅用一步预测估计策略梯度，从而降低计算和滚动误差。实现了基于流式数据的在线小批量策略梯度优化，并在模拟和真实机器人平台（Kinova Gen3机械臂、Unitree Go1四足机器人）上进行了验证。

Result: 方法在多个非线性控制基准和两个实际机器人硬件平台上均获得了比无模型RL算法更高的样本效率、比传统有模型RL算法更优的控制性能，且与依赖精确动力学模型的经典有模型方法控制表现相当。

Conclusion: 本文方法可有效提升非线性机器人控制的样本效率和控制性能，兼具理论创新与实际应用价值，为将Koopman动力学引入强化学习和机器人闭环控制提供了新思路。

Abstract: This paper presents a model-based reinforcement learning (RL) framework for optimal closed-loop control of nonlinear robotic systems. The proposed approach learns linear lifted dynamics through Koopman operator theory and integrates the resulting model into an actor-critic architecture for policy optimization, where the policy represents a parameterized closed-loop controller. To reduce computational cost and mitigate model rollout errors, policy gradients are estimated using one-step predictions of the learned dynamics rather than multi-step propagation. This leads to an online mini-batch policy gradient framework that enables policy improvement from streamed interaction data. The proposed framework is evaluated on several simulated nonlinear control benchmarks and two real-world hardware platforms, including a Kinova Gen3 robotic arm and a Unitree Go1 quadruped. Experimental results demonstrate improved sample efficiency over model-free RL baselines, superior control performance relative to model-based RL baselines, and control performance comparable to classical model-based methods that rely on exact system dynamics.

</details>


### [172] [Strain in Sound: Soft Corrugated Tube for Local Strain Sensing with Acoustic Resonance](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20017)
*Michael Chun,Ananya Nukala,Tae Myung Huh*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种新型软波纹管传感器，利用声学共振特性和机器学习算法，实现对管道分段应变的高精度估算，可区分软体物体的多关节形变。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 软体机器人和可穿戴设备对柔性、高分辨率的应变感知有强烈需求，现有传感器难以准确检测复合或非均匀形变。

Method: 设计了不同周期波纹的软管，当气流通过时激发声学共振，结合流速/频率数据和梯度提升回归算法，实现局部应变估算。实验通过不同拉伸条件下的共振数据训练算法。

Result: 双周期波纹管平均绝对误差为0.8 mm，单周期管为1 mm。在假手指模型上，可区分不同关节弯曲状态。

Conclusion: 该传感器能够准确估算软体结构的局部应变，适用于软体机器人和可穿戴系统，实现非均匀形变的检测。

Abstract: We present a soft corrugated tube sensor designed to estimate strain in each half segment. When air flows through the tube, the internal corrugated cavities induce pressure oscillations that excite the tube's standing wave resonance mode, generating an acoustic tone. Stretching the tube affects both the resonance mode frequency, due to changes in overall length, and the frequency-flow speed relationship, due to variations in cavity width, which is particularly useful for local strain estimation. By sweeping flow rates in a controlled manner, we collected resonance frequency data across flow speeds under various local stretch conditions, enabling a machine learning algorithm (gradient boosting regressor) to estimate segmental strain with high accuracy. The dual-period tube design (3.1 mm and 4.18 mm corrugation periods) achieved a mean absolute error (MAE) of 0.8 mm, while the single-period tube (3.1 mm) provided a satisfactory MAE of 1 mm. Testing on a mannequin finger demonstrated the sensor's capability to differentiate multi-joint configurations, showing its potential for estimating non-uniform deformations in soft bodies.

</details>

Abstract: Robotic autonomy in open-world environments is fundamentally limited by insufficient data diversity and poor cross-embodiment generalization. Existing robotic datasets are often limited in scale and task coverage, while relatively large differences across robot embodiments impede effective behavior knowledge transfer. To address these challenges, we propose JoyAI-RA, a vision-language-action (VLA) embodied foundation model tailored for generalizable robotic manipulation. JoyAI-RA presents a multi-source multi-level pretraining framework that integrates web data, large-scale egocentric human manipulation videos, simulation-generated trajectories, and real-robot data. Through training on heterogeneous multi-source data with explicit action-space unification, JoyAI-RA effectively bridges embodiment gaps, particularly between human manipulation and robotic control, thereby enhancing cross-embodiment behavior learning. JoyAI-RA outperforms state-of-the-art methods in both simulation and real-world benchmarks, especially on diverse tasks with generalization demands.

### [174] [Toward Safe Autonomous Robotic Endovascular Interventions using World Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20151)
*Harry Robertshaw,Nikola Fischer,Han-Ru Wu,Andrea Walker Perez,Weiyuan Deng,Benjamin Jackson,Christos Bergeles,Alejandro Granados,Thomas C Booth*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本研究提出并验证了一种基于世界模型（TD-MPC2）的自主机械取栓术导航方法，显示在多样化血管构型中具备优异的仿真和体外实验表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自主机械取栓术需要在高度多变的血管结构中实现精确、实时的导航控制，而当前基于强化学习的方法在不同患者解剖结构和复杂导航任务下健壮性有限。

Method: 采用基于世界模型的TD-MPC2（带有规划与动态学习的模型型强化学习）框架，针对多种导航任务进行训练，并与当前主流的SAC算法进行对比，分别在仿真和患者特异血管模型的体外实验（X线透视引导下）中进行评估。

Result: 在仿真中，TD-MPC2平均成功率（58%）显著高于SAC（36%），且触碰血管端部的平均力远低于血管破裂阈值。体外实验中，TD-MPC2的平均成功率（68%）与SAC（60%）相当，但路径选择更优（路径比更高），代价是操作时长更长。

Abstract: Autonomous mechanical thrombectomy (MT) presents substantial challenges due to highly variable vascular geometries and the requirements for accurate, real-time control. While reinforcement learning (RL) has emerged as a promising paradigm for the automation of endovascular navigation, existing approaches often show limited robustness when faced with diverse patient anatomies or extended navigation horizons. In this work, we investigate a world-model-based framework for autonomous endovascular navigation built on TD-MPC2, a model-based RL method that integrates planning and learned dynamics. We evaluate a TD-MPC2 agent trained on multiple navigation tasks across hold out patient-specific vasculatures and benchmark its performance against the state-of-the-art Soft Actor-Critic (SAC) algorithm agent. Both approaches are further validated in vitro using patient-specific vascular phantoms under fluoroscopic guidance. In simulation, TD-MPC2 demonstrates a significantly higher mean success rate than SAC (58% vs. 36%, p < 0.001), and mean tip contact forces of 0.15 N, well below the proposed 1.5 N vessel rupture threshold. Mean success rates for TD-MPC2 (68%) were comparable to SAC (60%) in vitro, but TD-MPC2 achieved superior path ratios (p = 0.017) at the cost of longer procedure times (p < 0.001). Together, these results provide the first demonstration of autonomous MT navigation validated across both hold out in silico data and fluoroscopy-guided in vitro experiments, highlighting the promise of world models for safe and generalizable AI-assisted endovascular interventions.

Our method translates natural-language safety regulations into executable predicates and deploys them through a redundant heterogeneous edge runtime. ### [176] [Stochastic Barrier Certificates in the Presence of Dynamic Obstacles](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20208)
*Rayan Mazouz,Luca Laurenti,Morteza Lahijanian*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种针对带有动态障碍物的随机动力系统的安全性分析方法，通过时间不变和时间变化的随机障碍函数，实现对有限时间内系统保持安全的概率下界的认证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在实际场景中，随机动力系统常面临障碍物动态变化带来的不确定性，如何有效评估和保证系统的安全性一直是难点，现有方法往往过于保守且计算复杂。

Method: 提出了时间不变和时间变化的随机障碍证书，将障碍物的时变性质纳入安全性分析。基于Bellman最优理论，有效整合时间结构，减少保守性。将证书限制为多项式，使得障碍函数的合成可转化为可解的凸和平方程序，提升实际可用性。

Result: 通过对有动态障碍的非线性系统进行实证验证，发现时间变化的障碍证书在安全概率下界保证上更紧致，且在精度和可扩展性方面优于现有方法。

Conclusion: 基于时间变化随机障碍证书的方法，显著提升了系统在动态障碍环境中安全概率评估的准确性和效率，并具备更好的实际应用价值。

Abstract: Safety of stochastic dynamic systems in environments with dynamic obstacles is studied in this paper through the lens of stochastic barrier functions. We introduce both time-invariant and time-varying barrier certificates for discrete-time, continuous-space systems subject to uncertainty, which provide certified lower bounds on the probability of remaining within a safe set over a finite horizon. These certificates explicitly account for time-varying unsafe regions induced by obstacle dynamics. By leveraging Bellman's optimality perspective, the time-varying formulation directly captures temporal structure and yields less conservative bounds than state-of-the-art approaches. By restricting certificates to polynomial functions, we show that time-varying barrier synthesis can be formulated as a convex sum-of-squares program, enabling tractable optimization. Empirical evaluations on nonlinear systems with dynamic obstacles show that time-varying certificates consistently achieve tight guarantees, demonstrating improved accuracy and scalability over state-of-the-art methods.

</details>

  <summary>Details</summary>

First, the system utility function is established on the basis of a general form of individual utility and its monotonic relationship, allowing for the simultaneous optimization of both individual and system objectives. Second, the Shapley value is introduced to compute each vehicle's marginal utility within the system, allowing its varying impact to be quantified. Finally, the HDV preference estimation is dynamically refined by continuously comparing the observed HDV behavior with the APG's estimated actions, leading to improvements in overall system safety and efficiency. Ablation studies demonstrate that adaptively updating Shapley values and HDV preference estimation significantly improve cooperation success rates in mixed traffic. Comparative experiments further highlight the APG's advantages in terms of safety and efficiency over other cooperative methods. Method: Cortex 2.0不再采取纯粹反应式决策，而是在视觉潜空间生成多个未来操作轨迹候选，并结合成功率和效率对这些轨迹进行打分，只执行最优候选。系统在单臂和双臂平台上，通过逐步提升难度的四项操控任务（如分拣、装箱拆箱等）进行了评估。

Conclusion: 基于世界模型的规划体系能显著提升工业机器人在复杂现实环境下的可靠性和泛化性，比传统反应式策略有明显优势。

Abstract: Industrial robotic manipulation demands reliable long-horizon execution across embodiments, tasks, and changing object distributions. While Vision-Language-Action models have demonstrated strong generalization, they remain fundamentally reactive. By optimizing the next action given the current observation without evaluating potential futures, they are brittle to the compounding failure modes of long-horizon tasks. Cortex 2.0 shifts from reactive control to plan-and-act by generating candidate future trajectories in visual latent space, scoring them for expected success and efficiency, then committing only to the highest-scoring candidate. We evaluate Cortex 2.0 on a single-arm and dual-arm manipulation platform across four tasks of increasing complexity: pick and place, item and trash sorting, screw sorting, and shoebox unpacking. Cortex 2.0 consistently outperforms state-of-the-art Vision-Language-Action baselines, achieving the best results across all tasks. These results demonstrate that world-model-based planning can operate reliably in complex industrial environments.

### [184] [Benefits of Low-Cost Bio-Inspiration in the Age of Overparametrization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20365)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 作者分别用CPG和MLP为控制器，以进化算法和强化学习协议进行训练，在同一机器人形态（具有限定本体感知能力）下，跨多种奖励函数，调整参数规模开展实验。引入“参数影响度”指标，分析参数数量和性能关系。

Result: 实验发现：浅层MLP和稠密连接的CPG在性能上优于深层MLP或Actor-Critic结构。参数影响度指标显示，强化学习所需增加的参数并未带来性能提升，反而支持了进化策略的优越性。

Conclusion: 在小规模输入输出和有性能上限的任务中，复杂化控制器结构并不带来更优效果；简单结构和进化训练更高效。参数空间的适度控制对机器人控制器优化至关重要。

Abstract: While Central Pattern Generators (CPGs) and Multi-Layer Perceptrons (MLP) are widely used paradigms in robot control, few systematic studies have been performed on the relative merits of large parameter spaces. In contexts where input and output spaces are small and performance is bounded, having more parameters to optimize may actively hinder the learning process instead of empowering it. To empirically measure this, we submit a given robot morphology, with limited proprioceptive capabilities, to controller optimization under two bio-inspired paradigms (CPGs and MLPs) with evolutionary- and reinforcement- trainer protocols. By varying parameter spaces across multiple reward functions, we observe that shallow MLPs and densely connected CPGs result in better performance when compared to deeper MLPs or Actor-Critic architectures. To account for the relationship between said performance and the number of parameters, we introduce a Parameter Impact metric which demonstrates that the additional parameters required by the reinforcement technique do not translate into better performance, thus favouring evolutionary strategies.

Motivation: 现有公开自动驾驶数据集缺乏真实车辆动态反馈与场景闭环交互，无法充分反映自动驾驶部署前的实际能力，限制了算法的验证和迭代。

Method: 针对上述问题，作者在2025 OnSite Autonomous Driving Challenge中采集了OVPD数据集，通过真实车辆环路测试，融合虚拟背景交通和车-路感知信息，实现了可控、可交互的闭环测试环境。数据集包含20个团队在15种基础场景下的测试数据，涵盖多模态、长时间序列的车辆轨迹、状态、控制指令和数字孪生视角数据。

Result: OVPD不仅支持对自动驾驶算法在特殊长尾场景中的规划与决策验证，还能实现开放式或平台级闭环评测，可多维度（安全、效率、舒适性、合规性、交通影响等）综合评估自动驾驶性能。

Conclusion: OVPD为自动驾驶测试和算法迭代提供了高保真、可重放和便于诊断的数据支持，提升了测试的严谨性和结果的可操作性，有助于推动自动驾驶部署落地。

Abstract: The rapid iteration of autonomous driving algorithms has created a growing demand for high-fidelity, replayable, and diagnosable testing data. However, many public datasets lack real vehicle dynamics feedback and closed-loop interaction with surrounding traffic and road infrastructure, limiting their ability to reflect deployment readiness. To address this gap, we present OVPD (OnSite Virtual-Physical Dataset), a virtual-physical fusion testing dataset released from the 2025 OnSite Autonomous Driving Challenge. Centered on real-vehicle-in-the-loop testing, OVPD integrates virtual background traffic with vehicle-infrastructure perception to build controllable and interactive closed-loop test environments on a proving ground. The dataset contains 20 testing clips from 20 teams over a scenario chain of 15 atomic scenarios, totaling nearly 3 hours of multi-modal data, including vehicle trajectories and states, control commands, and digital-twin-rendered surround-view observations. OVPD supports long-tail planning and decision-making validation, open-loop or platform-enabled closed-loop evaluation, and comprehensive assessment across safety, efficiency, comfort, rule compliance, and traffic impact, providing actionable evidence for failure diagnosis and iterative improvement. The dataset is available via: https://huggingface.co/datasets/Yuhang253820/Onsite_OPVD

</details>


### [186] [Lexicographic Minimum-Violation Motion Planning using Signal Temporal Logic](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20428)
*Patrick Halder,Lothar Kiltz,Hannes Homburger,Johannes Reuter,Matthias Althoff*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种可以高效应对自动驾驶车辆多重条件性冲突任务的最小违例运动规划方法，将复杂多目标优化转化为单目标问题，提升了计算效率和可解释性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自动驾驶运动规划时，经常会遇到无法同时满足所有约束（如安全、效率、舒适等）的问题；如何在不同优先级的需求之间权衡最小化违例，成为关键挑战。同时，如何高效进行高优先级约束下的优化也亟需改进。

Method: 本文利用信号时序逻辑(STL)对规划约束进行形式化，并将多目标字典序(lexicographic)优化通过非均匀量化和位移处理，转化为单目标标量优化。同时，扩展了确定性模型预测路径积分(MPPI)求解器，移除了对二次输入代价的需求。还引入了一种结合空间与时间约束的新谓词鲁棒性评估方法。

Result: 实验结果表明，提出的方法能高效、可扩展且可解释地在单目标求解框架下实现字典序STL最小违例运动规划，并有效兼顾多重约束优先级。

Conclusion: 转化后的方法不仅提高了运动规划求解器的效率，还提升了对形式化需求的可解释性和可扩展性，为复杂多约束场景下的自动驾驶运动规划提供了一种实用的解决途径。

Abstract: Motion planning for autonomous vehicles often requires satisfying multiple conditionally conflicting specifications. In situations where not all specifications can be met simultaneously, minimum-violation motion planning maintains system operation by minimizing violations of specifications in accordance with their priorities. Signal temporal logic (STL) provides a formal language for rigorously defining these specifications and enables the quantitative evaluation of their violations. However, a total ordering of specifications yields a lexicographic optimization problem, which is typically computationally expensive to solve using standard methods. We address this problem by transforming the multi-objective lexicographic optimization problem into a single-objective scalar optimization problem using non-uniform quantization and bit-shifting. Specifically, we extend a deterministic model predictive path integral (MPPI) solver to efficiently solve optimization problems without quadratic input cost. Additionally, a novel predicate-robustness measure that combines spatial and temporal violations is introduced. Our results show that the proposed method offers an interpretable and scalable solution for lexicographic STL minimum-violation motion planning within a single-objective solver framework.

Method: 设计了融合三种交互方式的多模态框架：1）运动引导型触觉操作用于精确空间修正；2）基于大语言模型（LLM）的安全自然语言适应（采用工具选择和参数化，不直接生成代码，以提升安全性）；3）图形化界面用于运动轨迹可视化及参数、路径编辑。整合了能量驱动的人意图检测、KMP运动编码、概率虚拟夹具及遍历控制等五大核心组件。

Abstract: Industrial robot applications require increasingly flexible systems that non-expert users can easily adapt for varying tasks and environments. ### [189] [Temporal Difference Calibration in Sequential Tasks: Application to Vision-Language-Action Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20472)
*Shelly Francis-Meretzki,Mirco Mutti,Yaniv Romano,Aviv Tamar*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种用于机器人视觉-语言-动作模型序列任务中的不确定性校准新方法，将Brier分数扩展到序列场景，并将不确定性校准与强化学习中的价值函数联系起来，实验显示该方法提升了模拟及真实机器人任务性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前VLA模型在机器人多步任务中不确定性量化很重要，但如何在只观测到部分轨迹情况下对最终成功概率进行可靠校准尚未得到充分研究。为解决这一痛点，作者提出对序列任务的不确定性校准进行系统性分析与改进。

Method: 作者定义了序列任务中的校准问题，引入了Brier分数的序列扩展，并通过理论推导，将最优校准目标与VLA策略的价值函数对齐，使强化学习中的时序差分（TD）价值估计成为进行不确定性校准的原则性方法。

Result: 实验证明，利用TD校准后，无论在模拟数据还是真实机器人实验中，模型性能都优于现有方法。此外，作者发现用TD校准后的单步动作概率也能给出具有竞争力的不确定性估计，挑战了前人结论。

Conclusion: 本研究为VLA模型在序列任务中的不确定性校准提供了理论路径和有效方法，通过价值函数校准可以显著提升任务绩效，拓宽了机器人强化学习与不确定性估计的接口。

Abstract: Recent advances in vision-language-action (VLA) models for robotics have highlighted the importance of reliable uncertainty quantification in sequential tasks. However, assessing and improving calibration in such settings remains mostly unexplored, especially when only partial trajectories are observed. In this work, we formulate sequential calibration for episodic tasks, where task-success confidence is produced along an episode, while success is determined at the end of it. We introduce a sequential extension of the Brier score and show that, for binary outcomes, its risk minimizer coincides with the VLA policy's value function. This connection bridges uncertainty calibration and reinforcement learning, enabling the use of temporal-difference (TD) value estimation as a principled calibration mechanism over time. We empirically show that TD calibration improves performance relative to the state-of-the-art on simulated and real-robot data. Interestingly, we show that when calibrated using TD, the VLA's single-step action probabilities can yield competitive uncertainty estimates, in contrast to recent findings that employed different calibration techniques.

### [190] [Passive Variable Impedance For Shared Control](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20557)
*Maximilian Mühlbauer,Nepomuk Werner,Ribin Balachandran,Thomas Hulin,João Silvério,Freek Stulp,Alin Albu-Schäffer*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在机器人共享控制中，合控方法通常利用阻抗控制来实现对目标位姿的引导，但实际应用中刚度系数和多目标间权重常常变化，导致传统方法在面对这些变量时难以保证系统稳定性，影响柔性和应用广度。该研究为了解决这一难题，提出统一处理的系统化策略，以应用于更灵活多变的合控场景。

Method: 作者针对阻抗控制中变量刚度和多控制器输出的加权仲裁提出了一套整体框架，将两者统一表达，并分析了系统被动性（passivity）受影响的机制，进而提出一套被动化（passivation）方法来消除稳定性隐患，使设计的刚度矩阵与仲裁因子均可为全矩阵且动态变化，提升方法通用性与灵活性。

Result: 提出的方法经仿真和实际机器人多场景实验验证，证明能稳定不同系统下的标准阻抗控制，有效适配各种需求，展现了优异的效果和行为多样性。

Conclusion: 该方法实现了对变量刚度和仲裁因子影响下的阻抗控制系统的稳定被动化，为开发更灵活且高效的机器人合控算法提供了理论与工程依据，对智能机器人领域具有重要应用价值。

Abstract: Shared Control methods often use impedance control to track target poses in a robotic manipulator. The guidance behavior of such controllers is shaped by the used stiffness gains, which can be varying over time to achieve an adaptive guiding. When multiple target poses are tracked at the same time with varying importance, the corresponding output wrenches have to be arbitrated with weightings changing over time. In this work, we study the stabilization of both variable stiffness in impedance control as well as the arbitration of different controllers through a scaled addition of their output wrenches, reformulating both into a holistic framework. We identify passivity violations in the closed loop system and provide methods to passivate the system. The resulting approach can be used to stabilize standard impedance controllers, allowing for the development of novel and flexible shared control methods. We do not constrain the design of stiffness matrices or arbitration factors; both can be matrix-valued including off-diagonal elements and change arbitrarily over time. The proposed methods are furthermore validated in simulation as well as in real robot experiments on different systems, proving their effectiveness and showcasing different behaviors which can be utilized depending on the requirements of the shared control approach.

### [191] [Kinematic Optimization of Phalanx Length Ratios in Robotic Hands Using Potential Dexterity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20686)
*HyoJae Kang,Joonho Lee,Jeongdo Ahn,Dong Il Park*

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种优化五指机器人手指骨节长度比例，提高其灵巧度的系统方法。通过多种指标综合评价，实现了不依赖具体操作任务的设计优化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在机器人手的设计阶段，骨节长度比例对手部灵巧度的影响难以定量评估，尤其在未定义具体操作对象或任务时更难以指导设计。

Method: 提出以“全球操作性”、“工作空间体积”、“重叠工作空间体积”和“指尖敏感性”为评估标准。采用权重目标函数，在给定约束下进行优化。通过体素化离散工作空间与均匀离散关节动作，对可达空间与性能指标进行评估，并在不产生操作空间重叠情形下，优化拇指及其他手指的长度比例组合。

Result: 发现各骨节对整体灵巧度贡献不均，分析了影响各骨节的重要因素。同时，不同性能指标在设计空间中的分布不均，调整权重系数并不总能直接带来单项性能提升。

Conclusion: 提出的框架实现了对机器人手指灵巧性、可达性与可控性之间权衡关系的系统化分析，为多指机器人机械手运动学设计提供了实用指导。

Abstract: In the design stage of robotic hands, it is not straightforward to quantitatively evaluate the effect of phalanx length ratios on dexterity without defining specific objects or manipulation tasks. Therefore, this study presents a framework for optimizing the phalanx length ratios of a five-finger robotic hand based on potential dexterity within a kinematic structure. The proposed method employs global manipulability, workspace volume, overlap workspace volume, and fingertip sensitivity as evaluation metrics, and identifies optimal design configurations using a weighted objective function under given constraints. The reachable workspace is discretized using a voxel-based representation, and joint motions are discretized at uniform intervals for evaluation. The optimization is performed over design sets for both the thumb and the other fingers, and design combinations that do not generate overlap workspace are excluded. The results show that each phalanx does not contribute equally to the overall dexterity, and the factors influencing each phalanx are identified. In addition, it is observed that the selection of weighting coefficients does not necessarily lead to the direct maximization of individual performance metrics, due to the non-uniform distribution of evaluation measures within the design space. The proposed framework provides a systematic approach to analyze the trade-offs among reachability, dexterity, and controllability, and can serve as a practical guideline for the kinematic design of multi-fingered robotic hands.

### [192] [FingerEye: Continuous and Unified Vision-Tactile Sensing for Dexterous Manipulation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20689)
*Zhixuan Xu,Yichen Li,Xuanye Wu,Tianyu Qiu,Lin Shao*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出FingerEye传感器：集成双目RGB摄像头实现近距离视觉和深度感知，接触后通过可变形弹性环结构结合标记点位姿估计，间接推算外力及力矩，从而实现视觉到触觉的连续感知流。配合多传感器融合的视觉—触觉模仿学习策略，并构建数字孪生体进行仿真和增广，使学习策略对物体变化更具泛化力。

Abstract: Dexterous robotic manipulation requires comprehensive perception across all phases of interaction: pre-contact, contact initiation, and post-contact. Such continuous feedback allows a robot to adapt its actions throughout interaction. However, many existing tactile sensors, such as GelSight and its variants, only provide feedback after contact is established, limiting a robot's ability to precisely initiate contact. We introduce FingerEye, a compact and cost-effective sensor that provides continuous vision-tactile feedback throughout the interaction process. FingerEye integrates binocular RGB cameras to provide close-range visual perception with implicit stereo depth. Upon contact, external forces and torques deform a compliant ring structure; these deformations are captured via marker-based pose estimation and serve as a proxy for contact wrench sensing. This design enables a perception stream that smoothly transitions from pre-contact visual cues to post-contact tactile feedback. Building on this sensing capability, we develop a vision-tactile imitation learning policy that fuses signals from multiple FingerEye sensors to learn dexterous manipulation behaviors from limited real-world data. We further develop a digital twin of our sensor and robot platform to improve policy generalization. By combining real demonstrations with visually augmented simulated observations for representation learning, the learned policies become more robust to object appearance variations. Together, these design aspects enable dexterous manipulation across diverse object properties and interaction regimes, including coin standing, chip picking, letter retrieving, and syringe manipulation. The hardware design, code, appendix, and videos are available on our project website: https://nus-lins-lab.github.io/FingerEyeWeb/

### [193] [A Kinematic Framework for Evaluating Pinch Configurations in Robotic Hand Design without Object or Contact Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20692)
*HyoJae Kang,Joonho Lee,Hyunmok Jung,Dong Il Park*

Main category: cs.RO

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有夹持能力评估方法过度依赖于物体几何或接触力模型，导致在机器人手设计早期难以评估其功能灵巧性，因此需要一种仅依赖运动学结构的方法。

Method: 先通过手指关节配置计算出各指尖的可达工作空间，再分析指尖对间的关系来检测可行的捏合配置，全过程不需物体或力学信息。

Abstract: Evaluating the pinch capability of a robotic hand is important for understanding its functional dexterity. However, many existing grasp evaluation methods rely on object geometry or contact force models, which limits their applicability during the early stages of robotic hand design. This study proposes a kinematic evaluation method for analyzing pinch configurations of robotic hands based on interactions between fingertip workspaces. First, the reachable workspace of each fingertip is computed from the joint configurations of the fingers. Then, feasible pinch configurations are detected by evaluating the relationships between fingertip pairs. Since the proposed method does not require information about object geometry or contact force models, the pinch capability of a robotic hand can be evaluated solely based on its kinematic structure. In addition, analyses are performed on four different kinematic structures of the hand to investigate their impact on the pinch configurations. The proposed evaluation framework can serve as a useful tool for comparing different robotic hand designs and analyzing pinch capability during the design stage.

### [194] [Visual-Tactile Peg-in-Hole Assembly Learning from Peg-out-of-Hole Disassembly](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20712)
*Yongqiang Zhao,Xuyang Zhang,Zhuo Chen,Matteo Leonetti,Emmanouil Spyrakos-Papastavridis,Shan Luo*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种结合视觉与触觉的新型方法，通过利用更易执行的反向任务（拔出插头）来加速和优化插入装配任务的学习。在多个插孔场景下验证了新框架的有效性，显著提升了效率和成功率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统插入装配任务在机器人领域具有重要意义，但主要面临探索空间大、对齐精度高等挑战。强化学习虽有前景，但实际应用受限于数据效率低和样本收集困难。因此，研究如何高效利用数据、提升插入任务学习质量，成为一个亟需解决的问题。

Method: 作者构建了一个统一的视觉-触觉观测环境，将插入（PiH）和拔出（PooH）都形式化为部分可观测马尔可夫决策过程（POMDPs）。首先，通过在PooH任务上训练策略，收集包含运动、视觉和触觉信息的轨迹，并对这些轨迹进行时间反转和动作扰动，作为插入任务的专家数据。最终，结合视觉用于定位接近，触觉用于对齐补偿，共同实现高效学习。

Result: 实验结果显示，该视觉-触觉融合策略在多种不同孔型下表现优异，相比单一模态策略，插入力减小6.4%，在已见与未见物体上的插入成功率分别达87.5%与77.1%，比从零强化学习提升18.1%。

Conclusion: 结合视觉和触觉信息、以拔出任务反哺插入难题，极大提升了装配智能体的泛化能力和数据效率，为机器人装配领域带来突破性的进展。

Abstract: Peg-in-hole (PiH) assembly is a fundamental yet challenging robotic manipulation task. While reinforcement learning (RL) has shown promise in tackling such tasks, it requires extensive exploration. In this paper, we propose a novel visual-tactile skill learning framework for the PiH task that leverages its inverse task, i.e., peg-out-of-hole (PooH) disassembly, to facilitate PiH learning. Compared to PiH, PooH is inherently easier as it only needs to overcome existing friction without precise alignment, making data collection more efficient. To this end, we formulate both PooH and PiH as Partially Observable Markov Decision Processes (POMDPs) in a unified environment with shared visual-tactile observation space. A visual-tactile PooH policy is first trained; its trajectories, containing kinematic, visual and tactile information, are temporally reversed and action-randomized to provide expert data for PiH. In the policy learning, visual sensing facilitates the peg-hole approach, while tactile measurements compensate for peg-hole misalignment. Experiments across diverse peg-hole geometries show that the visual-tactile policy attains 6.4% lower contact forces than its single-modality counterparts, and that our framework achieves average success rates of 87.5% on seen objects and 77.1% on unseen objects, outperforming direct RL methods that train PiH policies from scratch by 18.1% in success rate. Demos, code, and datasets are available at https://sites.google.com/view/pooh2pih.

</details>


### [195] [ALAS: Adaptive Long-Horizon Action Synthesis via Async-pathway Stream Disentanglement](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20721)
*Yutong Shen,Hangxu Liu,Lei Zhang,Penghui Liu,Yinqi Liu,Liuxiang Yang,Tongtong Feng*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种仿生学启发的跨域长时序任务学习框架ALAS，有效提升了人-场景交互中多步任务的泛化与效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有长时序任务方法依赖于将预训练子技能串联，不能很好地泛化到新环境与技能组合，难以完成跨域的人-场景交互复杂任务。

Method: 受大脑“where-what”双通路机制启发，提出ALAS框架，通过环境学习模块与技能学习模块，实现环境-自我、技能-运动的解耦，有效提升跨域与跨技能泛化能力。环境学习模块用于捕捉空间与语义信息，实现环境自我解耦；技能学习模块关注自身运动模式，实现运动结构独立编码。

Result: 在多个人-场景交互长时序任务上，ALAS较现有方法子任务成功率平均提升23%，执行效率提升29%。

Conclusion: ALAS实现了复杂人-场景任务中跨域、跨技能的泛化和高效执行，对长时序任务具有显著推动作用。

Abstract: Long-Horizon (LH) tasks in Human-Scene Interaction (HSI) are complex multi-step tasks that require continuous planning, sequential decision-making, and extended execution across domains to achieve the final goal. However, existing methods heavily rely on skill chaining by concatenating pre-trained subtasks, with environment observations and self-state tightly coupled, lacking the ability to generalize to new combinations of environments and skills, failing to complete various LH tasks across domains. To solve this problem, this paper presents ALAS, a cross-domain learning framework for LH tasks via biologically inspired dual-stream disentanglement. Inspired by the brain's "where-what" dual pathway mechanism, ALAS comprises two core modules: i) an environment learning module for spatial understanding, which captures object functions, spatial relationships, and scene semantics, achieving cross-domain transfer through complete environment-self disentanglement; ii) a skill learning module for task execution, which processes self-state information including joint degrees of freedom and motor patterns, enabling cross-skill transfer through independent motor pattern encoding. We conducted extensive experiments on various LH tasks in HSI scenes. Compared with existing methods, ALAS can achieve an average subtasks success rate improvement of 23\% and average execution efficiency improvement of 29\%.

</details>


### [196] [A Hough transform approach to safety-aware scalar field mapping using Gaussian Processes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20799)
*Muzaffar Qureshi,Trivikram Satharasi,Tochukwu E. Ogri,Kyle Volle,Rushikesh Kamalapurkar*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种无人机器人在未知危险环境下安全高效地测绘标量场的方法。通过高斯过程和霍夫变换，机器人能实时推断危险区域并避开高风险区，实现安全采样和路径规划。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 环境中存在危险（标量场值高于阈值），直接人工测绘不安全，因此需要自主机器人进行安全、高效的数据采集和区域测绘。

Method: 将标量场建模为高斯过程，通过贝叶斯推断获得均值和不确定性；用霍夫变换实时估计高风险区域空间结构，根据高斯过程后验概率提供的安全概率，规划机器人的安全采样点和运动路径。

Result: 方法在两个数值仿真和一个室内光强场实验证明有效，实现了机器人对危险区域的规避和高效标量场测绘。

Conclusion: 基于高斯过程和霍夫变换的安全采样与规划策略，提升了机器人在高风险未知环境中的测绘能力，实验结果证实方法的有效性和实用性。

Abstract: This paper presents a framework for mapping unknown scalar fields using a sensor-equipped autonomous robot operating in unsafe environments. The unsafe regions are defined as regions of high-intensity, where the field value exceeds a predefined safety threshold. For safe and efficient mapping of the scalar field, the sensor-equipped robot must avoid high-intensity regions during the measurement process. In this paper, the scalar field is modeled as a sample from a Gaussian process (GP), which enables Bayesian inference and provides closed-form expressions for both the predictive mean and the uncertainty. Concurrently, the spatial structure of the high-intensity regions is estimated in real-time using the Hough transform (HT), leveraging the evolving GP posterior. A safe sampling strategy is then employed to guide the robot towards safe measurement locations, using probabilistic safety guarantees on the evolving GP posterior. The estimated high-intensity regions also facilitate the design of safe motion plans for the robot. The effectiveness of the approach is verified through two numerical simulation studies and an indoor experiment for mapping a light-intensity field using a wheeled mobile robot.

</details>


### [197] [PokeVLA: Empowering Pocket-Sized Vision-Language-Action Model with Comprehensive World Knowledge Guidance](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20834)
*Yupeng Zheng,Xiang Li,Songen Gu,Yuhang Zheng,Shuai Tian,Weize Li,Linbo Wang,Senyu Fei,Pengfei Li,Yinfeng Gao,Zebin Xing,Yilun Chen,Qichao Zhang,Haoran Li,Wenchao Ding*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为PokeVLA的新型视觉-语言-动作(VLA)模型，通过两阶段训练范式，有效提升了机器人操作的效率、知识集成和空间感知。实验证明在多个基准和真实部署下均取得领先性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有VLA方法在机器人操作中存在效率低、缺乏高级知识与空间感知等问题，限制了机器人在复杂环境中的实用性。本文旨在提升机器人操作的智能化水平。

Method: 采用两阶段训练：首先使用240万多模态样本预训练紧凑的视觉-语言模型(PokeVLM)，涵盖空间定位、可供性和具身推理等任务；其次通过多视角目标感知语义学习、几何对齐以及创新动作专家，将与操作相关的表征注入动作空间。

Result: 在LIBERO-Plus基准和实际机器人部署中均表现优越，成功率和抗干扰性超越现有同类方法，具备更强的鲁棒性和泛化性。

Conclusion: PokeVLA能够以轻量高效的方式，将视觉-语言理解能力注入机器人动作决策，大幅提升机器人操作水平。代码、模型权重及相关数据集脚本将开源，推动社区研究进展。

Abstract: Recent advances in Vision-Language-Action (VLA) models have opened new avenues for robot manipulation, yet existing methods exhibit limited efficiency and a lack of high-level knowledge and spatial awareness. To address these challenges, we propose PokeVLA, a lightweight yet powerful foundation model for embodied manipulation that effectively infuses vision-language understanding into action learning. Our framework introduces a two-stage training paradigm: first, we pre-train a compact vision-language model (PokeVLM) on a curated multimodal dataset of 2.4M samples encompassing spatial grounding, affordance, and embodied reasoning tasks; second, we inject manipulation-relevant representations into the action space through multi-view goal-aware semantics learning, geometry alignment, and a novel action expert. Extensive experiments demonstrate state-of-the-art performance on the LIBERO-Plus benchmark and in real-world deployment, outperforming comparable baselines in success rate and robustness under diverse perturbations. To foster reproducibility and community progress, we will open-source our code, model weights, and the scripts for the curated pre-training dataset. Project page: https://getterupper.github.io/PokeVLA

</details>
